<date>1616715584226< /date><Rating>5</Rating><Review>I am the physician-grandmother of a teenage boy with acne, relocating his care from SF to the East Bay.  I was pleased with Dr. Icecreamwala's assessment of his skin condition (basically providing a second opinion, and concurring with the previous provider's thinking).  I appreciated her careful discussion about the pros and cons of Acutane.  Given the possible  side effect of serious depression, she advised waiting with a trying this medication until post-pandemic return to normal life.    During the pandemic it would be  difficult to judge whether depression could be caused by the pandemic's disruptions in a young person's life,  or whether it was likely an Acutane side effect.  Without our being able to 'know' which was causing the depression, Acutane would have to be stopped since causation couldn't be ruled out.  Dr. Icecreamwala  added that once Acutane was stopped because it MIGHT have caused depression, doctors would likely be unwilling to try it (again) in the future.
So, in a careful and caring way she gave us serious food for thought, related well to our young-adult grandson, and provided him a positive encounter even though he was disappointed that she did not encourage use of Acutane at this point in time.< /Review><pictures>None</pictures>< resp>

<Text>If you want to catch the seals, go here during the day. They come out to bask in the sun. They also come out later in the evening. However, then the lighting is low and you can hardly get much. Pretty neat watching them during the day though. Plenty of photography opportunities. They're there even in winters - in fact, esp during winter months. Tourists are few to come by. So you get better opportunities to work your camera on the sea creatures!<//Text>< pictures>

< Review>
This is one of four holes that are in the dock surrounded by a railing for you to look down into to see the Sea lions. This port hole is the closed to the end of the dock. There are three more after it going back to the shore. It really is a fun way to look at the wild life and see the lazy sea lions taking their naps.< /Review>

< review>
Fair pricing, good selection and good service - trustworthy.

I have done business with U Sav-Mor over the last 10 years.  I have found them to be both professional and knowledgeable.  As  a professional painter with experience in technical coatings as well as automotive finishes in restorations, detail is important to me and have found that I can get the information that I need to help me make a wise decision when selecting materials that I may not have experience with or a material for a special application.

I can understand why they ask for paint codes.  For those who complain - just because you don't understand doesn't mean that they are wrong.  Depending on when the car was built in any given year there can be more than one paint color that looks similar - You can't just say I need the light blue color for 2015 - there can be more than one shade that looks similar depending on when the car was built.  They can't be mixing paint based on what you think the color is.  If you are wrong they pay for it not you so they should ask if you have the paint code - automotive paint is expensive.

This store can be very busy and someone who is trying to help multiple people at one time may seem like they are rude when all they are is busy and you just take it the wrong way.  Personally I get it.  Sometimes my favorite person there doesn't have the time and I have to wait my turn,  call back or wait for them to call me back - BUT they always call back!   Maybe some people are the type that offend easily - I am not.

I can buy paint and materials from anyone that I want to.  I have accounts with other suppliers.  I choose to do business with Sav-Mor because they can be trusted.

Beware of negative reviews - I found that looking at a few of the negative reviewers complain a lot about everyone - I think you have to consider the source or read between the lines to see if they are just unhappy people in general with nothing to contribute< /review>
